    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<span id="freeTextContainer5087301619680779315">A mansion full of secrets…<br/>From the moment investigative reporter Jackie Alexander steps foot inside the mansion dominating the Demiris estate on the beautiful Greek island of Corfu, her suspicions are on high alert. This is no ordinary assignment… The life of her beloved cousin, Aphrodite, is in grave danger, as the heirs to the incredible fortune of Greek tycoon Andreas D</span>
  <span id="freeText5087301619680779315" style="display:none">A mansion full of secrets…<br />From the moment investigative reporter Jackie Alexander steps foot inside the mansion dominating the Demiris estate on the beautiful Greek island of Corfu, her suspicions are on high alert. This is no ordinary assignment… The life of her beloved cousin, Aphrodite, is in grave danger, as the heirs to the incredible fortune of Greek tycoon Andreas Demiris die one after the other, under mysterious circumstances…<br /><br />A man with secrets of his own…<br />The only person who can help Jackie is Michael Apostolou, former Special Forces Officer and one of the finest detectives on the Athens police force. Soon enough though, Jackie realizes, that despite her simmering desire for him, she can’t really trust him, as the seductive detective seems to be investigating those mysterious deaths for reasons of his own…<br /><br />Trusting the wrong person can be deadly…<br />Jackie and Michael are forced to work together, but the suspicions and unanswered questions are devouring them, just like their rising passion for each other. In games like this, the stakes are high and the players are ruthless… When Jackie is kidnapped by the most dangerous player of all, time is running out, as Michael is forced to choose between jeopardizing his mission and personal quest for justice, or the life of the gorgeous intruder of his heart…</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/946786763?book_show_action=true">May 24, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Becky ♡The Bookworm♡" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Becky ♡The Bookworm♡" href="/user/show/29318167-becky-the-bookworm">Becky ♡The Bookworm♡</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer946786763" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8556920115140496459">I hate giving bad reviews, but this 1/2 star book needed a LOT of work. A beta reader would've been a great help in fixing the confusing plot. There were so many nondescript characters and names that half the time I didn't know who was who, or what in the world was going on. Half the dialogue was ridiculous, meaningless filler. The other half was overdramatic and forced. I was tempted to start a drinking game every time I read <i>"What now?"</i> <br/><br/>I never did understand what Jackie hoped to accomplish by</span>
  <span id="freeText8556920115140496459" style="display:none">I hate giving bad reviews, but this 1/2 star book needed a LOT of work. A beta reader would've been a great help in fixing the confusing plot. There were so many nondescript characters and names that half the time I didn't know who was who, or what in the world was going on. Half the dialogue was ridiculous, meaningless filler. The other half was overdramatic and forced. I was tempted to start a drinking game every time I read <i>"What now?"</i> <br /><br />I never did understand what Jackie hoped to accomplish by visiting the mansion on her uncle's behalf. If she was trespassing and worried about being caught by the police, why did she bring food to stock the fridge and plan to stay a few days? Note that she does this just after a miraculous recovery from a car wreck. This is just one example of the conflicting information contained in the book. I understand that she wants to find the man responsible for killing the Demiris heirs, as does Michael, but Jackie was hopelessly stupid and repeatedly walked directly into danger. Don't get me started on how many times she swooned and fainted away from the stress she put herself through. <br /><br />I actually felt a little sorry for Michael having to save her ... over and over and over. The romance was non-existent and the law enforcement came across like the Keystone Cops. The action was unrealistic and everything moved WAY too fast. As a reader I need a chance to breathe and absorb what's happening. This story is written like a bad fanfic and I was really disappointed. From the summary, I had expected so much better. Thankfully I only spent 99 cents on it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8556920115140496459" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4498308414785732643">Loved the book!!!<br/><br/>I downloaded “Spellbound in your arms” looking for wonderful novel, intrigued by the title and the beautiful book cover.   <span id="freeText4498308414785732643" style="display:none">Loved the book!!!<br /><br />I downloaded “Spellbound in your arms” looking for wonderful novel, intrigued by the title and the beautiful book cover. I fell in love with Angel Sefer’s novel. She has a wonderful writing style and the plot was extremely appealing. <br /><br />She interweaves with an amazing skill, mystery, danger, romance and a lot of unexpected twists and turns. I would highly recommend this book to anyone who loves a good mystery. <br /><br />The story takes place on a beautiful Greek Island. Jackie a beautiful investigative reporter and Michael a very attractive detective find themselves thrown together in this intriguing plot, trying to solve a murder that has put the heirs to an incredible fortune of Greek Tycoon Andreas Demiris in gave danger. <br /><br />I was totally captivated and drawn to the story like a magnet. I just couldn’t put the book down. I was charmed by the amazing job Anger Sefer did to help you feel the emotions of her characters and keep you glued to the pages. <br /><br />The simmering desire that develops between Jackie and Michael is wonderful. It is a real page-turner. At the end of the story I found myself wanting more…I am hoping there is another book coming from the same author. <br /></span>

<div id="review_662147605" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/662147605" />
    <a title="Joe Prentis" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2711868-joe-prentis"><img alt="Joe Prentis" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442465882p2/2711868.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/662147605?book_show_action=true">Jul 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Joe Prentis" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Joe Prentis" href="/user/show/2711868-joe-prentis">Joe Prentis</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer662147605" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13972619198035291985">Spellbound in His Arms by Angel Sefer<br/><br/><br/>When I was growing up, I could not wait for the next Helen MacInnes novel to appear on the shelves of our school library. When I discovered Spellbound by Angel Sefer I realized I had found another author who had the ability to blend romance, mystery and an interesting location into a captivating plot. <br/><br/>The main character in Spellbound is an investigative reporter named Jackie Alexander, who travels from Atlanta to Greece to investigate a dangerous and puzzling</span>
  <span id="freeText13972619198035291985" style="display:none">Spellbound in His Arms by Angel Sefer<br /><br /><br />When I was growing up, I could not wait for the next Helen MacInnes novel to appear on the shelves of our school library. When I discovered Spellbound by Angel Sefer I realized I had found another author who had the ability to blend romance, mystery and an interesting location into a captivating plot. <br /><br />The main character in Spellbound is an investigative reporter named Jackie Alexander, who travels from Atlanta to Greece to investigate a dangerous and puzzling mystery. Her visit to the Demiris estate on the Island of Corfu, immediately plunges her into jeopardy. Jackie needs to examine some documents locked away in the mansion, but encounters an intruder on her arrival at the isolated estate. The intruder is Michael Apostolou, a police detective, who has the same intentions as Jackie, but apparently for a different reason. Jackie and Michael are instantly attracted to each other, but there are too many unanswered questions to allow them to trust each other. <br /><br />This book is fast paced, but surprisingly easy to read. I found myself racing through the pages, then scrolling back to reread and savor each twist and turn in the plot. The geographic details supply just the right amount of information to make you aware of the exotic surroundings without slowing down the flow of the story. Romance, suspense, and mystery supply the reader with an interesting combination that is hard to beat. Five stars from me for a story well done. This debut novel from Ms Sefer is one you don’t want to miss. I am looking forward to many others as this series continues.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13972619198035291985" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Christoph Fischer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13998364-christoph-fischer"><img alt="Christoph Fischer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473825343p2/13998364.jpg" /></a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christoph Fischer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christoph Fischer" href="/user/show/13998364-christoph-fischer">Christoph Fischer</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition 9781620152157" href="/book/show/20936206-spellbound-in-his-arms">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer781921571" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16086271301920826955">"Spellbound in His Arms" by Angel Sefer is a great romantic suspense story set on the beautiful Greek island of Corfu. The story throws the reader in at the deep end with investigative reporter Jackie Alexander being caught breaking and entering in a mansion while trying to find information about a series of 'accidents'. The suspicious events are eliminating heirs to a family fortune in Greece and Jackie's wants to prevent further deaths by taking matters in her own hand.<br/>Caught by the very attra</span>
  <span id="freeText16086271301920826955" style="display:none">"Spellbound in His Arms" by Angel Sefer is a great romantic suspense story set on the beautiful Greek island of Corfu. The story throws the reader in at the deep end with investigative reporter Jackie Alexander being caught breaking and entering in a mansion while trying to find information about a series of 'accidents'. The suspicious events are eliminating heirs to a family fortune in Greece and Jackie's wants to prevent further deaths by taking matters in her own hand.<br />Caught by the very attractive detective Michael Apolstolou she soon joins forces with him but the relationship between them remains 'complicated'.<br />The story is written so smoothly and well paced that I hardly noticed the time passing. The chemistry between the characters is right there from the start but Sefer has thankfully added a few more threads to the complex plot to keep readers intrigued and involved beyond the romance story.<br />With a love for detail the author describes the life of the rich, the corrupt and the powerful, the evil doers and their intrigues, distrust and often unhappy lives.<br />Romance and mystery lovers are being served well here with great suspense and a strong romance between the two main characters taking centre stage in an exciting and passionate crime novel.<br />Great entertainment.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16086271301920826955" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/874797855?book_show_action=true">Mar 07, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="M.M. Jaye" class="user" itemprop="url" name="M.M. Jaye" href="/user/show/20286570-m-m-jaye">M.M. Jaye</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition 9781620152157" href="/book/show/20936206-spellbound-in-his-arms">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20286570-m-m-jaye?shelf=well-paced">well-paced</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20286570-m-m-jaye?shelf=instant-attraction">instant-attraction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20286570-m-m-jaye?shelf=feisty-heroine">feisty-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20286570-m-m-jaye?shelf=original-settings">original-settings</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20286570-m-m-jaye?shelf=detective-story">detective-story</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20286570-m-m-jaye?shelf=sweet-romance">sweet-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20286570-m-m-jaye?shelf=greek-setting">greek-setting</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer874797855" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4559224101874786537">I finished reading "Spellbound in his Arms" in a single day. Trust me, that was not my intention. My very busy schedule allows me to read while I commute to work and just a bit in bed, before my eyes slide shut and my Kindle hits me on the nose. Well, that wasn't the case here. I stayed up well after my usual bedtime because I just had to finish this riveting story. Angel Sefer weaves an intricate story full of twists, turns, mistrust and unexpected surprises that come down in a torrent from the</span>
  <span id="freeText4559224101874786537" style="display:none">I finished reading "Spellbound in his Arms" in a single day. Trust me, that was not my intention. My very busy schedule allows me to read while I commute to work and just a bit in bed, before my eyes slide shut and my Kindle hits me on the nose. Well, that wasn't the case here. I stayed up well after my usual bedtime because I just had to finish this riveting story. Angel Sefer weaves an intricate story full of twists, turns, mistrust and unexpected surprises that come down in a torrent from the very first page! The reader has barely time to pause and breathe in the intoxicating bougainvillea aromas or take in the wonderful Corfiat scenery, and yet another gunshot makes investigative reporter Jackie Alexander take flight. Most of the times though, she runs right into gorgeous detective's Michael Apostolou's arms. If only she could be sure where he stands in this web of manipulative, deadly heirs and their victims that keep adding up.<br /><br />If you enjoy suspenseful romances set against an exotic island setting, "Spellbound in his Arms" is just the book for you. Note: this is a sweet romance.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4559224101874786537" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_951262580" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/951262580" />
    <a title="Siddiqru" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27497163-siddiqru"><img alt="Siddiqru" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1413754035p2/27497163.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/951262580?book_show_action=true">May 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Siddiqru" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Siddiqru" href="/user/show/27497163-siddiqru">Siddiqru</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition 9781620152157" href="/book/show/20936206-spellbound-in-his-arms">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27497163-siddiqru?shelf=wtf-did-i-just-read">wtf-did-i-just-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27497163-siddiqru?shelf=was-expecting-more">was-expecting-more</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer951262580" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12072077022518753454">I'm <b>
  <i>so</i>
</b> frustrated with this book! <b>***DO NOT TRUST HIGH RATINGS</b><br/><a href='http://photobucket.com/images/getting%20mad' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398295340ra/9396559.gif' alt='getting mad photo: mad photo12.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Ok no seriously what on earth is going on with these 5 star ratings? There are many books where I see a high rating, so give it a shot, and then realize its probably a case of <i>its not you it's me</i>. However this is definitely not the case. Something is seriously going on here with the amount of people that gave this a high rating, and every time someone rates it poorly, another high rating gets added. If you don't think that fis</span>
  <span id="freeText12072077022518753454" style="display:none">I'm <b>
  <i>so</i>
</b> frustrated with this book! <b>***DO NOT TRUST HIGH RATINGS</b><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/getting%20mad" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398295340ra/9396559.gif" alt="getting mad photo: mad photo12.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ok no seriously what on earth is going on with these 5 star ratings? There are many books where I see a high rating, so give it a shot, and then realize its probably a case of <i>its not you it's me</i>. However this is definitely not the case. Something is seriously going on here with the amount of people that gave this a high rating, and every time someone rates it poorly, another high rating gets added. If you don't think that fishy as hell, I don't know what is.<br><br>Moving onto the story itself. This book as a whole I think was written poorly and story wasn't executed properly. Am I being harsh? Definitely, but I have to be straightforward when it comes to my reviews. I'd rather be honest then add fluff to mislead people. Trust me if you want a good review, don't look far, I'm sure theres one right below or above mine <i>(*note the sarcasm)</i>. The main reason I picked this book up was because I was feeling a little bit of romantic suspense at the moment. In all good suspense novels, there is a case to solve and the story gradually builds up until you discover who's the culprit. However in this book there was no way to even guess what was going on, because the story was all over the place. The two main characters, Michael and Jackie had no chemistry whatsoever and there was barely any romance. Their whole relationship was just weird. It was neither insta-love or a gradual build-up, it was just there if that makes sense. Now onto the heroine, I assumed she would be bad-ass because of her spirit and drive to help her family solve a mystery, but instead her character kept throwing herself in stupid situations that required her to be saved. <br><br>Overall I didn't connect with the characters or the story, and I think the author needs to execute her work with a little more thought. My intent isn't too bash the author, because writing a book in itself is hard work, but its not her writing or story that is ticking me off. Its these damn ratings that are misleading people to buy a book. I'm just taking a guess, i'm not sure if this is the case, but I'm going to venture and say a "street team" is behind this. A street team is a group of followers the author has, that keep rating his or her books with high ratings, which throws off the balance of what honest people are reviewing and writing. This has been more common in the book world, and I think its just sad that people are resorting to stuff like this to get people to buy their books. Its not fair and disappointing. Maybe there really is no street team, but I know for a fact something weird is going on with the amount of high ratings there are.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12072077022518753454" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer12863265089507932337">I know you shouldn't judge a book its cover, but I fell for this book when I first saw it anyway. I love how the author describes the characters falling in love at first sight. I completely believe in this and have experienced it myself.   <span id="freeText12863265089507932337" style="display:none">I know you shouldn't judge a book its cover, but I fell for this book when I first saw it anyway. I love how the author describes the characters falling in love at first sight. I completely believe in this and have experienced it myself. It's a wonderful feeling that is difficult to capture, but the author does it well. This book also made me fall in love with Corfu, the Greek Island where the hero and heroine spend on a roller coaster ride of kidnapping, passion, daring escapes, and searching for hidden treasure.<br /><br />I found the romance and thrills blended well together. It's not always easy to write a book that appeals to both romance fans and people who enjoy a good mystery/thriller, but I think the author pulled it off. I'm looking forward to reading more in the Greek Isles Series.</span>

<div id="review_1136358893" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1136358893" />
    <a title="Hazel *Craves the Angst Reviews*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6848917-hazel-craves-the-angst-reviews"><img alt="Hazel *Craves the Angst Reviews*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1381252112p2/6848917.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hazel *Craves the Angst Reviews*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hazel *Craves the Angst Reviews*" href="/user/show/6848917-hazel-craves-the-angst-reviews">Hazel *Craves the Angst Reviews*</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1136358893" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer13427903885835081357">Find This and Other Reviews At <a href='http://cravestheangst.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Craves The Angst</a>.<br/><br/><u>Spellbound In His Arms</u> is book one in <i>The Greek Isles Series</i> and is a Romance, Suspense written by <i>Angel Sefer</i>. I was gifted a copy from Sarka at <i>
  <a href='http://booktrope.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Booktrope Publishing</a>
</i> in exchange for an honest review.<br/><br/><b>3 “Perfect Afternoon Read” Stars!</b><br/><br/>Jackie Alexander is on a mission to find a killer before the killer finds her cousin. Using her investigative reporting background, she travels to the Demiris Mansion on the island of Corfu in search of papers that </span>
  <span id="freeText13427903885835081357" style="display:none">Find This and Other Reviews At <a href="http://cravestheangst.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Craves The Angst</a>.<br /><br /><u>Spellbound In His Arms</u> is book one in <i>The Greek Isles Series</i> and is a Romance, Suspense written by <i>Angel Sefer</i>. I was gifted a copy from Sarka at <i>
  <a href="http://booktrope.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Booktrope Publishing</a>
</i> in exchange for an honest review.<br /><br /><b>3 “Perfect Afternoon Read” Stars!</b><br /><br />Jackie Alexander is on a mission to find a killer before the killer finds her cousin. Using her investigative reporting background, she travels to the Demiris Mansion on the island of Corfu in search of papers that may determine the outcome of a fortune as well as expose clues to the name of the person who is killing off the Demiris aires. <br /><br />But on a dark, cold night, the last thing she expected to find in a secluded, abandoned mansion was a handsome stranger who pulls on some deep and unfamiliar emotion inside her. However, knowing who to trust isn’t easy with a killer on the loose.<br /><br />Detective Michael Apostolou is ex-special forces turned cop and is investigating the deaths that surround the Demiris inheritance. People are dropping like flies and he needs to get to the bottom of it before the next victim. But upon meeting the beautiful Jackie, he might just have more to lose than he ever thought possible... and it doesn’t help that neither of them are being honest. <br /><br />He has secrets. She has secrets. And as they hide from their instant attraction, the killer closes in and no one is safe.<br /><br />The author did a great job of building a very suspenseful and thrilling mystery. You know right off where the conflict is coming from but there are surprises along the way you don’t see coming and that was fun.<br /><br />This read was short, fast paced and exciting. There wasn’t a dull moment.. however, I think that some of the scenes were TOO fast. This read was filled with lots of mystery and lots of actual story but there wasn’t a lot of passion or romance. The characters fell in insta-love and there was no slow build. Also, the ending felt rushed. The characters seemed to walk on scene, quickly play their parts and just as quickly, exit stage left. There were no emotions in the telling of it, no descriptive words to enhance the feelings of the scene and not much dialogue. It was more like a “telling” of events and I’m more of a lover of “showing” the events. And their was very little character development.<br /><br />Overall, this was a wonderful mystery with exciting action, interesting developments, suspenseful events and an enchanting setting. I loved the beautiful and eerie feel of the island and the mansion. I do wish there had been more development with the characters and more passion/romance but regardless, this was a good, quick afternoon read.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13427903885835081357" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5354126371456553115">This book LITERALLY sucked me in with the very first paragraph!!! Look farther down to get a peek at it!! :-)<br/> <br/>This book was page after page of constant action! Seriously, check out the very first paragraph of this book:<br/> <br/> <br/>Beging excerpt - Jackie stopped dead in her tracks. What was that? A light noise coming from somewhere in the back of the mansion turned her blood to ice. She immediately turned the flashlight off and stood still, holding her breath. Her mouth went dry. What if there was someone</span>
  <span id="freeText5354126371456553115" style="display:none">This book LITERALLY sucked me in with the very first paragraph!!! Look farther down to get a peek at it!! :-)<br /> <br />This book was page after page of constant action! Seriously, check out the very first paragraph of this book:<br /> <br /> <br />Beging excerpt - Jackie stopped dead in her tracks. What was that? A light noise coming from somewhere in the back of the mansion turned her blood to ice. She immediately turned the flashlight off and stood still, holding her breath. Her mouth went dry. What if there was someone in the mansion? How would she explain who she was and what she was doing here in the middle of the night? Then again, would her explanations make any difference to whomever, or even worse whatever, was out there? The old mansion was pitch black, far away from any civilized soul and the owner dead. Who could it be? - end excerpt<br />~ Chapter 1, Paragraph 1, Spellbound in His Arms<br /> <br />I’m not sure I can tell you how very much I enjoyed this book! It really was fly by the seat of your pants! Every time things finally calmed down for Jackie – BAM – she was off and running again! It was so much fun! I like the ways that Michael finds her and helps her. Because is could have very easily been redundant, but each time he was able to was a totally different circumstance. Sometimes it was easy, sometimes not. <br />I had a very hard time putting this book down because it is so action packed! It is not a super long book, but it just flew by. I couldn’t believe how much happened and I don’t think she wasted a single word! J I think very few authors would be able to pack that much into a book and make it believable. Of course I was rolling my eyes at Jackie a couple times and thinking “uh-oh, here she goes again!”, but the events were such that I believed she had no choice.<br /> <br />The bottom line – get this book, you won’t regret it. It was a fun book and a little like your favorite roller coaster. Two people falling in love, yet they don’t quite trust each others…..hmmmm…..LOVE IT!! Feel free to read more at my blog <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://joecoolreview.com">http://joecoolreview.com</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/676906279?book_show_action=true">Jul 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carolyn Aspenson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carolyn Aspenson" href="/user/show/19770946-carolyn-aspenson">Carolyn Aspenson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer676906279" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17043791716495545068">I'm up for reading anything with a setting in a country to which I've traveled. I loved Corfu so that location for starters, drew me in. <br/><br/>This is a great read for anyone who likes romance/mysteries. The mystery part of the plot was well written and carried the story. The setting wasn't so much in Corfu as it was in an old mansion in Corfu but the author did a good job at making me feel as if I was there. <br/><br/>The love story part of this book is does exactly what it's supposed to do...it creates a fant</span>
  <span id="freeText17043791716495545068" style="display:none">I'm up for reading anything with a setting in a country to which I've traveled. I loved Corfu so that location for starters, drew me in. <br /><br />This is a great read for anyone who likes romance/mysteries. The mystery part of the plot was well written and carried the story. The setting wasn't so much in Corfu as it was in an old mansion in Corfu but the author did a good job at making me feel as if I was there. <br /><br />The love story part of this book is does exactly what it's supposed to do...it creates a fantasy of which so many women want...love at first site. Michael immediately falls for Jackie, a connection he felt because of her appeal to his eyes. I love the fantasy of that but know that kind of love, for me is very much not reality. Do I believe in love at first site? No, but that's exactly why I like to read about it. <br /><br />I don't read books to learn about far away places. I don't read books to be educated (unless of course that is their job). I read books to be taken to another place, to be a fly on the wall of a fictional life, to watch it weave a web and find an ending. If you read books for similar reasons, this is a lovely read and completely does that. <br /><br />The book was well written and I believe can be read by people who don't have strong reading or comprehension skills. I don't normally put something like that in a review but for this book I think it's important to point it out. Why? Because while the book has some twists and turns, it's an easy read and wouldn't overwhelm someone who might struggle with words. The writer doesn't use big words in unnecessary places to prove she's a writer. That, for me, makes it a good read for anyone who needs an escape. </span>
  <a data-text-id="17043791716495545068" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText8602896411500006092" style="display:none">Stephanos (Uncle) had once mentioned to Jackie Alexander that something supernatural was responsible for the mysterious drowning deaths in the family of Greek tycoon Constantinos, Andreas (cliff), Demiris &amp; Dimitris Apostolou. He also instructed her to seek out an attorney over there. The couple had 2 girls Maria &amp; Aphrodite. Jackie’s parents were killed in a plane crash &amp; she was taken in by her uncle/aunt. Stephanos &amp; Martha (uncle/aunt) &amp; Maria were now dead also. <br />Jackie is bound &amp; determined to find out the clues on her own on who/how/why the Demiris family members are ending up dead. <br /><br />Detective Tony Mavrikis setting at a restaurant (Plaka) gets an expected visit from a female. <br /><br />Will Philip Manos get what he wants? Lots of interesting scenarios &amp; a great host of characters to keep track of. This could make a great spine chilling romantic crime movie or TV series. No doubt in my mind a very easy rating of 5 stars for this book. <br />Thank you for the free book <br />Tony Parsons MSW (Washburn)<br /></span>

<div id="review_674716831" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/674716831" />
    <a title="Caroline Fardig" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18784027-caroline-fardig"><img alt="Caroline Fardig" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474639584p2/18784027.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/674716831?book_show_action=true">Jul 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Caroline Fardig" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Caroline Fardig" href="/user/show/18784027-caroline-fardig">Caroline Fardig</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer674716831" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5345371137914874056">SPELLBOUND IN HIS ARMS is a fantastic first novel by author Angel Sefer. Set in Greece, mostly on the island of Corfu, with some scenes in Athens (I was excited to find a short scene took place in Plaka, a historic neighborhood in Athens and my favorite spot when I vacationed there!). The author describes the Greek scenery beautifully (she is from there, after all), and the location is definitely a major player in the story.<br/><br/>The chemistry between the main characters, Jackie and Michael, is fiery </span>
  <span id="freeText5345371137914874056" style="display:none">SPELLBOUND IN HIS ARMS is a fantastic first novel by author Angel Sefer. Set in Greece, mostly on the island of Corfu, with some scenes in Athens (I was excited to find a short scene took place in Plaka, a historic neighborhood in Athens and my favorite spot when I vacationed there!). The author describes the Greek scenery beautifully (she is from there, after all), and the location is definitely a major player in the story.<br /><br />The chemistry between the main characters, Jackie and Michael, is fiery and passionate right from the start, but what I really liked is that they were able to keep their heads to solve the mystery even as their relationship blossomed. Jackie is a feisty heroine, and nothing, even super-hot detective Michael Apostolou, is going to keep her from finding the truth about who is harming her family. There are plenty of bad guys and plenty of action in this book—perfect for a fast and fun read.<br /><br />I would highly recommend this book to anyone who likes a good mystery with a good amount of romance. I look forward to reading more novels by this author.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5345371137914874056" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5904639142008668495">Spellbound In His Arms intrigued me from the beginning, and it held me captivated as I turned each page. I enjoyed the way the author kept the plotline moving along nicely, and the twists at the end threw me for a loop! Jackie and Michael seemed to fall in love from the start when they met, which I will not delve into because that would ruin the plot. While I'm not normally the type of reader to fall in love with the characters from the beginning, I found that I was rooting for them the entire w</span>
  <span id="freeText5904639142008668495" style="display:none">Spellbound In His Arms intrigued me from the beginning, and it held me captivated as I turned each page. I enjoyed the way the author kept the plotline moving along nicely, and the twists at the end threw me for a loop! Jackie and Michael seemed to fall in love from the start when they met, which I will not delve into because that would ruin the plot. While I'm not normally the type of reader to fall in love with the characters from the beginning, I found that I was rooting for them the entire way through the novel.<br /><br />There were times that I was very frustrated with Jackie for acting irrationally, but it did not ruin the story for me. In fact, I enjoyed the way that she had a few flaws, at least, things that might be considered flaws to me.<br /><br />As a synopsis, I would say that this book is an excellent mystery and romance novel that has a little bit of thriller sprinkled throughout. It kept me on my toes as I was reading. In fact, it only took me two sittings to actually read this, and only because I had to do laundry! </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3648943835257136367"><b>ABHA'S REVIEW<br/><br/>3.5 STARS</b><br/><br/>I would summarize “Spellbound in His Arms” in one word: exciting! This was a fun easy read that had it all; romance, excitement and mystery with Corfu for the backdrop of the story. Jackie flies down to the Greek island to get to the bottom of all the murders in Andreas Demiris’ family. There are definitely a lot of twists and turns. Michael and Jackie are thrown into situations that get the adrenaline flowing. <br/><br/>There are a lot of chases, near deaths and escapes. The book de</span>
  <span id="freeText3648943835257136367" style="display:none"><b>ABHA'S REVIEW<br /><br />3.5 STARS</b><br /><br />I would summarize “Spellbound in His Arms” in one word: exciting! This was a fun easy read that had it all; romance, excitement and mystery with Corfu for the backdrop of the story. Jackie flies down to the Greek island to get to the bottom of all the murders in Andreas Demiris’ family. There are definitely a lot of twists and turns. Michael and Jackie are thrown into situations that get the adrenaline flowing. <br /><br />There are a lot of chases, near deaths and escapes. The book definitely keeps you turning the pages, and trying to find the answer. Primarily, the book is about finding love and helping one’s family. Some of the situations are too magnificent to take seriously. They seem far-fetched and that’s one of the reasons why I give this book three and a half stars. <br /><br />Overall, this is a fun book and a quick read. A good one for a long trip for sure. <br /></span>

  <span id="freeText17968036494175073374" style="display:none">Investigative reporter Jackie Alexander travels to Corfu, Greece and pokes around the Demiris mansion in the middle of the night, hoping to find out what’s behind the string of murders in her family. Enter Michael, a hot Grecian police detective, and the sparks begin to fly.<br/><br/>Spellbound in His Arms is a great addition to the romantic suspense genre. Readers of J.D. Robb and Maggie Shayne will love this book!</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/724229505?book_show_action=true">Sep 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lillian Mackenzie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lillian Mackenzie" href="/user/show/15153187-lillian-mackenzie">Lillian Mackenzie</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer724229505" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17753920833302082003">Spellbound In His Arms was a very intriguing suspense romance, the first I have ever read, and it did not disappoint. The breathtaking Michael Apostolou and the energetic, bombshell Jackie Alexander kept me excited with each twist and turn of the story.<br/><br/>The story centers around Jackie Alexander looking for answers to the mysterious murder of her cousin Maria Demiris. With the bitter consent of her uncle Stephanos, we find her in the deserted mansion of Constantinos Demiris searching for a safe fu</span>
  <span id="freeText17753920833302082003" style="display:none">Spellbound In His Arms was a very intriguing suspense romance, the first I have ever read, and it did not disappoint. The breathtaking Michael Apostolou and the energetic, bombshell Jackie Alexander kept me excited with each twist and turn of the story.<br /><br />The story centers around Jackie Alexander looking for answers to the mysterious murder of her cousin Maria Demiris. With the bitter consent of her uncle Stephanos, we find her in the deserted mansion of Constantinos Demiris searching for a safe full of important papers but the only thing she finds is the gorgeous Detective Michael Apostolou instead. The two receive an attractive spark for each other immediately, but soon find out that they have other dangerous matters to attend to before they can get acquainted. Phillip Manos and his diabolical son Eric being the first on the villain hit list. With the help of a few supporting characters and bullet spraying chases, the couple finds the answers to all of their questions that plagued them.<br /><br />I loved the suspense aspect of this read. By 40 percent, I had to know what was going on with the murders. Every time this brilliant writer would reveal a pivotal answer, she would unveil yet another mystery which left me biting my nails on my quest to get to the answers. The angst felt by the two leads drove me batty wanting him to finally take her to his bed and make lengthy passionate love to her, but there was no time because proverbial fires needed distinguishing.<br /><br />This is a great suspenseful read and for anyone looking for a juicy chase, mystery, and romance, this is the Greek romance for you.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17753920833302082003" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_764996818" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/764996818" />
    <a title="Jonel" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15432163-jonel"><img alt="Jonel" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1476629586p2/15432163.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/764996818?book_show_action=true">Nov 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jonel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jonel" href="/user/show/15432163-jonel">Jonel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer764996818" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11760859814235262386">This novel was intensely real. Every event was not only possible but extremely plausible. As a reader you get caught up in the suspense of the story while rooting for the budding romance. The entire story was written in a realistic yet completely captivating light. Her narrative in natural and fluid, simultaneously filling the reader in and keeping them guessing. Sefer’s descriptions paint a brilliant picture of this Greek isle, combining romanticism with reality to create a phenomenal whole. <br/><br/>Th</span>
  <span id="freeText11760859814235262386" style="display:none">This novel was intensely real. Every event was not only possible but extremely plausible. As a reader you get caught up in the suspense of the story while rooting for the budding romance. The entire story was written in a realistic yet completely captivating light. Her narrative in natural and fluid, simultaneously filling the reader in and keeping them guessing. Sefer’s descriptions paint a brilliant picture of this Greek isle, combining romanticism with reality to create a phenomenal whole. <br /><br />The cast of characters in this novel was fantastically developed. Sefer uses a sliding scale of development for each character based on their role in the story. It adds for a very unique feel. I also appreciate how you get to know the male lead as the female lead does. The gradual character development adds an air of mystery to this brilliant alpha male. The female lead was the only real issue that I had with this story. I mean really... How stupid can you be? That said, I also loved her as a lead. She just made a few decisions that had me wanting to smash my head off the wall. <br /><br />Suspense and intrigue definitely play a role in this intriguing tale with some very romantic vibes. I’d definitely recommend it to anyone who enjoys the genre. <br /><br />Please note that I received this novel free of charge from the author in exchange for an honest review.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11760859814235262386" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_730222908" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/730222908" />
    <a title="Daphne Bois" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18994250-daphne-bois"><img alt="Daphne Bois" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1553261329p2/18994250.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/730222908?book_show_action=true">Sep 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Daphne Bois" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Daphne Bois" href="/user/show/18994250-daphne-bois">Daphne Bois</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer730222908" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4915470375657614706">If you’re looking for romance, a great story and perfect escapism, this book is ideal. I’ve never read a romantic thriller before this, but I will definitely read more now. The author combines a hot romance with a thrilling adventure mystery, and it definitely makes for a great story. I was caught up in the story right from the start – Jackie is exactly the kind of heroine I enjoy reading about. She doesn’t just sit back and wait to things to happen to her. She gets out there and gets things don</span>
  <span id="freeText4915470375657614706" style="display:none">If you’re looking for romance, a great story and perfect escapism, this book is ideal. I’ve never read a romantic thriller before this, but I will definitely read more now. The author combines a hot romance with a thrilling adventure mystery, and it definitely makes for a great story. I was caught up in the story right from the start – Jackie is exactly the kind of heroine I enjoy reading about. She doesn’t just sit back and wait to things to happen to her. She gets out there and gets things done: she’s clever, proactive and tough. And Michael is just downright swoon-worthy. <br /><br />The description of the Greek islands is also truly gorgeous. You can really tell that the author loves her setting and she manages to capture it with such skill that you truly get transported into a world of blue seas, glorious beaches and ancient mansions.<br /><br />I really liked Jackie and Michael as a pairing – the chemistry between them was really hot right from the start – and who wouldn’t want to solve family mysteries and face danger accompanied by a handsome, clever Greek detective? Especially one with his own mysterious past!<br />This is a very exciting start for a new series and I can’t wait to read the other books as they come out!<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5064963765439249671">Investigative reporter Jackie Alexander travels to Corfu, Greece and pokes around the Demiris mansion in the middle of the night, hoping to find out what’s behind the string of murders in her family. She doesn’t expect to run into detective Michael Apostolou, though, who has his own agenda for being in the mansion in the dead of night. Then there’s physical attraction, kidnappings, shootouts and intrigue that kept me reading late into the night.<br/><br/>Sefer’s romantic suspense story kept me on the edge</span>
  <span id="freeText5064963765439249671" style="display:none">Investigative reporter Jackie Alexander travels to Corfu, Greece and pokes around the Demiris mansion in the middle of the night, hoping to find out what’s behind the string of murders in her family. She doesn’t expect to run into detective Michael Apostolou, though, who has his own agenda for being in the mansion in the dead of night. Then there’s physical attraction, kidnappings, shootouts and intrigue that kept me reading late into the night.<br /><br />Sefer’s romantic suspense story kept me on the edge of my seat and was hard to put down. There were lots of twists and turns, so I was never sure who to trust and what was going to happen next. I can’t wait to read another book by this author.<br /></span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13906581885225356213">I like romance and I love mysteries, so I was intrigued by the blurb. I also liked the fact that the novel takes place on the beautiful Greek island of Corfu. The book was a refreshing, wonderful surprise. I thoroughly enjoyed reading this fantastic book and highly recommend it. <br/><br/>Mystery and magic blended with romance and adventure created a very interesting plot and I kept on turning pages. The characters were fascinating and I am looking forward for the next book in the series...<br/></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Opq/xpqubQ97ZOuBaqkKHJFMVjP9gTuezveJAU5GaDMAvNYUIfCkZ9xPX+CdXADDRxOx+zMMtfmVic+wgwWaqQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('smvl4sqqxkCWHEp329Qrfwy+c2Z/VqnVefHUMKg9kiGITYwwcfQPKDE3/hYsISGg2uGUrrHbJ7Iij5KBZX5guw==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer9769681504366037491">Multiple award-winning, bestselling author Angel Sefer was born in Athens, Greece, and has studied and worked on both sides of the Atlantic. She holds a degree in Economics and divides her time between the corporate world and her real passion: writing mystery, thriller, and suspense romances where passion flares and danger lurks around every corner.<br/><br/>Angel lives in Athens, Greece, with the two loves</span>
  <span id="freeText9769681504366037491" style="display:none">Multiple award-winning, bestselling author Angel Sefer was born in Athens, Greece, and has studied and worked on both sides of the Atlantic. She holds a degree in Economics and divides her time between the corporate world and her real passion: writing mystery, thriller, and suspense romances where passion flares and danger lurks around every corner.<br /><br />Angel lives in Athens, Greece, with the two loves of her life - her son and her husband - and is a member of several writers groups.<br /><br />The Greek Islands - alluring destinations that cast a spell on the visitor from the very first moment - are among her favorite settings. She has written a series of standalone mystery romance novels - The Greek Isles Series - each taking place on a different island.<br /><br />In this series, dark mysteries mingle with sizzling romances, while the exquisite beauty of the enchanting Greek Islands will steal the reader’s heart away.<br /><br />Angel has also written a collection of novellas full of passion, danger, and intrigue - The Alluring Love Collection.<br /><br />Fascinated by the concepts of soul mates and reincarnation - the eternal cycles of the soul between this world and the Other Side - Angel has started a new paranormal romance collection, cloaked in mystery and suspense—The Flames of Destiny Collection.<br /></span>
